The post went live at 11:38 p.m. on July 16, and just 20 minutes later the rogue employee in question was brought to the attention of the Burger King in question. At least I hope he's a villain. How did it happen? Well, the BK employee hadn't removed the Exif data from the uploaded photo, which indicated the culprit was somewhere in Mayfield Heights, Ohio. That was at 11:47 a.m. Three minutes later, at 11.50 a.m., the address of the Burger King branch was published with the wish for happy unemployment. 5 minutes later the news channel was contacted by another 4channer. And three minutes later, at 11:58 am, a link was posted: BK's Tell Us About Us online forum. The foot photo, also known as exhibit A, was attached. Cleveland Scene Magazine contacted the BK the next day. When asked, the breakfast shift supervisor said: "Oh, I know who that is. He's going to be fired." Mystery solved by 4chan. Now we can all eat our fast food in peace again.
